# 실종 아동 찾기 원문 로그

**Gamemaster:** 여러분은 의뢰를 받아 변경 지역의 고난이도 던전을 답파한 뒤, 이제 막 오리진으로 돌아가는 길입니다.

**Gamemaster:** 던전의 먼지와 피 냄새가 아직 장비에 남아 있을 오후 무렵, 여러분은 작은 마을에 도착합니다.

**Gamemaster:** 마을은 예상과 달리 떠들썩하군요.

**Gamemaster:** 광장에는 색색의 깃발이 걸려 있고, 아이들은 입사귀 모양 과자를 들고 뛰어다닙니다.

**엘테라 마스테:** "어라…축제…?"

**소녀:** 부모들은 아이의 머리를 빗겨주며 신전 쪽으로 향하고 있습니다.

**라비니아:** "과자…!"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "아이들이 많군. 좋은 현상이다."

**민간인 남성:** 지나가는 길에 한 포장마차 주인이 여러분들의 행색을 보더니 말을 걸어옵니다

**민간인 남성:** "외지인들이신가?"

**라비니아:** "아핫, 그렇습니다요…!"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "맞다."

**라비니아:** "야생의 모험가인겁니다요"

**네모(Nemo):** (네모는 어째서인지 오늘만큼 어린 엘프가 되었습니다. 1년에 한번씩 어린 아이인 모습으로 된다는군요)"이래뵈어도 모험가에요!"

**엘테라 마스테:** "아…네. 던전에서 일을 마치고 돌아오는 길인데…뭔가 축제 분위기네요"

**민간인 남성:** "보아하니 힘든 싸움을 하고 왔나본데, 언제나 우리의 평화를 위해 힘써주셔서 고맙소."

**민간인 남성:** "이런 시기에 온 것도 다 인연인데, 과자 좀 받으시구랴."

**라비니아:** "그렇다면…!"

**라비니아:** "감사히받겠습니다요!"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 슬쩍 받아들더니, 코로 냄새를 킁킁 맡는다.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "독이 있나?"

**엘테라 마스테:** @과자를 먹어본 적이 거의 없기에 당황스러워 하는군요

**라비니아:** 하고 와다다닷 하고 달려가서 받아 입안에 넣습니다

**민간인 남성:** 구수하고 달콤한 향이 나는 바삭한 과자로군요

**라비니아:** @레로레로레로레로

**카구야:** "어머. 감사해요. 친절하셔라~."

**네모(Nemo):** "아저씨, 전 어린 아이인 만큼 많이 주세요!"(나이 속이기 참 쉽다

**엘테라 마스테:** "…그렇게 혀로 먹는게…아닌 것 같은데요…"

**민간인 남성:** "그래그래. 어린데도 열심히구나!"

**라비니아:** "…!"

**민간인 남성:** 네모에게는 특별히 커다란 녀석으로 쥐어주는군요

**네모(Nemo):** "와아! 아저씨 최고!"

**민간인 남성:** "하하하! 그러냐!"

**엘테라 마스테:** @그럼 라비니아가 들고 있던 과자 하나를 먹어보니 바삭한 식감에 묘한 맛으로 느껴지는군요.

**민간인 남성:** "아참, 그러고보니 무슨 축제냐고 물어보셨었나?"

**엘테라 마스테:** @과자를 먹다가 "아…네."

**네모(Nemo):** "네! 무슨 축제에요?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "맛있군. 음. 음." 우물거린다.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "더 줘라."

**네모(Nemo):** "정 원하시면 제거 드세요"

**민간인 남성:** "오늘은 경사스러운 날이지. 세계수님의 가호를 받을 수 있는지 아닌지 아이들의 적성을 검사하는 날이오."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "세계수…"

**민간인 남성:** "2~3 년에 한번씩 열리다보니 사제님들이 적성을 봐주는 며칠간이 축제처럼 되었지."

**카구야:** "아하. 제가 살던 곳에서도 비슷한 날이 있었답니다."

**네모(Nemo):** "오오, 재밌겠는데요?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 네모의 것을 받아들고 오도독 오도독 씹어먹으며 생각한다.

**엘테라 마스테:** "적성…검사라…"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "전사의 자질을 시험하는 날인가."

**민간인 남성:** "음~ 그렇게도 볼 수 있겠구려."

**라비니아:** "헤에"

**라비니아:** "라비니아는 라비니아가 바라는대로 세계수의 가호를 받을수 있어서 다행이었습니다요"

**엘테라 마스테:** "가호라도 받을 수 있다면…어느 누구에게나 좋을테니까…그걸 바라는 의미로 축제를 열고 있었다면 이해는 되네요"

**네모(Nemo):** "아저씨, 어디서 볼 수 있어요? 궁금해요"

**민간인 남성:** "교회로 가면 될 거요."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "적성이 뛰어난 차기 전사들을 노린다든가 하는 일은 없나? 모험가가 필요한…" 새로 얻은 검을 과시하듯 꺼내며…

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "그런 일 말이지." 히죽 웃는다.

**민간인 남성:** 이리의 말에 민간인 남성이 놀리는 표정을 짓습니다

**민간인 남성:** "우리 동네는 예로부터 안개에 위협을 많이 받아서 그런가. 비슷한 전래동화가 있네."

**민간인 남성:** "이맘때면 가호를 받아야할 아이들이 안개에게 잡혀간다는 이야기지."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "안개라…"

**네모(Nemo):** "안개요? 그럼 그 아이들은 어떻게 되나요?"

**민간인 남성:** "영영 사라지는거지 어떻게 되겠소."

**민간인 남성:** "무시무시하지?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "안개는 베는 맛이 없다."

**엘테라 마스테:** "…안개 내부엔 그 무엇도 없다고 들었어요…특히 가호가 있다고 해도…위험할지도요"

**엘테라 마스테:** "음…그럼, 여러분. 한번 그 교회로 가볼까요…? 이 마을에서 쉬어야한다면 적어도 축제가 어떻게 되는지는 한번 보고 싶네요…"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "좋다. 차기 전사를 보는 일은 기꺼운 일이지."

**네모(Nemo):** "좋아요! 교회로 가서 한번 검사 받아보고 싶어요"

**민간인 남성:** 여러분이 그렇게 노점을 떠나려고 할 때 즈음

**라비니아:** "라비니아는 새로운걸 익히는게 좋습니다요"

**민간인 남성:** 뒤에서 작은 체구가 여러분에게 떨리는 목소리로 말을 겁니다.

**여사제 - 에리나:** "저, 저기. 모험가님들. 피곤하실텐데 죄송합니다만…"

**카구야:** "저도 이 곳의 축제를 구경해보고 싶네요~. 어라? 누구신가요?" @목소리를 향해 고개를 돌린다.

**네모(Nemo):** "네?!"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "크릉?"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "혹시 키가 요만한 갈색머리 하프엘프 소녀를 못 보셨나요?"

**라비니아:** "?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "유괴인가?"

**네모(Nemo):** "엘프라면 저긴 한데, 하프엘프는 잘 모르겠어요"

**엘테라 마스테:** "여기로 오면서 그런 꼬마는…못 봤습니다만"

**엘테라 마스테:** "혹시 무슨 일이라도…?"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "그게, 오늘 아침에 자고 일어나니 홀연히 사라져버려서… 오늘 내내 찾고 있는데도 안 보여요."

**여사제 - 에리나:** "다른 곳 같으면 그냥 축제날이니 아침 일찍 놀러 나갔겠거니 싶었는데.

**여사제 - 에리나:** "예전부터 흉흉한 전설이 도는 마을이라 혹시 몰라서 찾고 있는데도 안보이지 뭐에요…."

**라비니아:** "그걸 본 다른 사람은 아예 없던겁니까요?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "그 아이의 이름이 뭐지?"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "마리아입니다. 고아원에서 제일 나이가 많아서 방을 혼자 쓰고 있어서 본 사람은… 없는거 같더군요."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "마리아… 이름, 기억했다."

**네모(Nemo):** "흠, 기억을 한번 되짚어 보도록 하죠"(저희가 이 마을에 온 뒤에, 여사제가 말한 외형의 아이를 본 적이 있을까요?)

**Gamemaster:** 지나가는 아이들이 워낙 많아 헷갈리지만 아직 본 적은 없는거 같군요

**네모(Nemo):** "헷갈리긴 한데, 본 적은 없는 것 같아요"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "만약 도와주신다면 제가 드릴 수 있는 선에서 보상해드릴게요…!"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "어떻게 안될까요?"

**엘테라 마스테:** "음…그럼 그 아이가 평소에 가는 곳이라던가…아니면 뭔가 수상쩍은 점은 없었나요?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "교회는 가 보았나? 오늘 같은 날이라면 홀로 교회에 갔을지도 모르지."

**여사제 - 에리나:** "가는 곳은 다 찾아봤지만 없었습니다. 그리고 특이할 점은… 가호 적성이 있다고 밝혀져서 어제 밤 늦게까지 깨있었던걸로 기억해요."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "호오."

**라비니아:** "그거 설마 자기 과신으로 안개 속으로 간거 아닙니까요..?""

**네모(Nemo):** "혹시 마나흔같은게 느껴지나요? 느껴진다면 마법 계열의 사람들이 납치했을 거 같은데…"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "그, 그럴리가요! 위험하다고 엄하게 가르쳤는데!"

**라비니아:** "원래 아이들은 다들 자신감이 넘치는겁니다요"

**여사제 - 에리나:** 네모의 말에 마법을 쓸 수 있는 아니라고 답변합니다

**카구야:** "알겠습니다. 마을을 돌아다니다가 찾으면 저희가 보호할게요."

**라비니아:** (바바구나..

**엘테라 마스테:** @곰곰히 생각하다가 "…그렇다면…그 아이가 있었던 방으로 안내 해줄 수 있으신가요…?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "찾은 뒤에는 어디로 가면 되지?"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "정말 감사합니다. 발견하시면 고아원으로 데리고 와주세요."

**여사제 - 에리나:** 엘테라의 말에 "…괜찮으시다면 안내해드릴까요?"

**네모(Nemo):** (마법을 쓸 수 있는 아니라고 답변이 마법 못 쓴다는거죠?)

**엘테라 마스테:** "네. 그 쪽에서 마을 내부를 뒤져봤는데도 못 찾았다면…어린 아이의 움직임으로는 불가능 하다는 생각 밖에 들지 않아서요…"

**여사제 - 에리나:** (넹 마법을 못 쓰니 마법흔적도 없을것

**네모(Nemo):** (어쩌지 흠

**엘테라 마스테:** "제 생각이지만…저희가 마을을 뒤져도 결과는 같을지도요"

**네모(Nemo):** "안내해 주실 수 있을까요? 단서는 언제나 현장에 있는 법이죠"

**엘테라 마스테:** "그렇다면, 그 아이가 처음 있었던 곳에서부터 알아내는 수 밖에 없을 것 같아요…"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "설마 아이들을 납치하는 나쁜 사람들이 있다는 말씀이신가요?!"

**엘테라 마스테:** "최악의 경우라면…네."

**여사제 - 에리나:** "이 좋은 사람들 중에 그런 인간말종이 있을 리 없는데…"

**네모(Nemo):** (잠깐만

**네모(Nemo):** "잠시만 기다려 주세요"

**엘테라 마스테:** "…?"

**네모(Nemo):** Chancellor 발동!
이 카드를 뽑은 후 8시간 이내에, 물질 구성 요소 없이 행동으로 점술(Augury) 주문을 한 번 시전할 수 있습니다. 지능, 지혜 또는 매력 중 하나를 주문 시전 능력치로 사용하십시오.

**네모(Nemo):** (아이는 누군가에 의해 납치당한 것인가요?)

**엘테라 마스테:** (그걸…점술로 물을 수 있는가?

**Gamemaster:** 네

**네모(Nemo):** "큰일 났습니다. 그 소녀 납치되었습니다"

**카구야:** (점술은 좋다 아니다만 나오긴 하니까

**네모(Nemo):** "제 점술 주문에 의하면 누군가에 의해 납치되었다고 나옵니다. 시간이 없습니다"

**카구야:** (납치당한 기준으로 찾으면 되는가 질문으로 해석하면 가능하긴 할 듯?

**여사제 - 에리나:** "그, 그런…"

**엘테라 마스테:** "…."

**여사제 - 에리나:** 휘청거리면서 쓰러질뻔 하는군요

**라비니아:** (yes or no로 대답할수 있는건

**라비니아:** (답해주긴함

**네모(Nemo):** (주문 썼으니 d20굴리기

**네모(Nemo):** 18
1d20 = 18 = 18

**엘테라 마스테:** "…문제라면, 그 납치가 어디서, 누구에 의해 되었는지를 몰라요"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "부, 부탁드립니다! 모험가 여러분! 반드시 사례할테니 마리아를 찾아주세요!"

**엘테라 마스테:** "결국은 그 마리아 라는 꼬마가 있던 곳으로…가봐야 할 것 같네요"

**여사제 - 에리나:** "당장 안내해드릴게요…!"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "차기 전사의 적성을 노린 건가… 그렇다면 그 차기 전사의 적성은 정확히 어떤 능력이었지?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "하나하나 단계를 밟아보자고."

**네모(Nemo):** "경비대에게 납치 사건이라고 말해주세요. 그럼 안내해주세요"

**여사제 - 에리나:** 마음이 앞서서 치맛자락을 밟고 넘어질뻔 하는군요

**카구야:** "걱정하지 마세요. 저희가 반드시 마리아를 안전하게 돌려보내 드릴게요." @넘어질 뻔하는 에리나를 잡아주며

**네모(Nemo):** Innate Sorcery Feature

You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

Choose a willing creature that you can see within range. Until the spell ends, the target’s Speed is doubled, it gains a +2 bonus to Armor Class, it has Advantage on Dexterity saving throws, and it gains an additional action on each of its turns. When the spell ends, the target is Incapacitated and has a Speed of 0 until the end of its next turn, as a wave of lethargy washes over it.

**카구야:** Bardic Inspiration Feature
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Action 1 hour 60 ft 1 creature

**카구야:** Inspired Eclipse Feature
When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

Pneumatic Strike. After you make an attack roll with this weapon, but before the result of the attack is determined, you can use a bonus action to pull the blade’s trigger. With a pneumatic thrust, the top of the weapon arcs forward and you gain a +4 bonus to the attack roll.
Tetanus Blade. When you hit a creature with an attack that uses Pneumatic Strike, the pathogens that live within the rusty blade are reinvigorated by its magic, and the attack deals an additional 4 (1d8) Poison damage.Backfire. When you roll an 8 on Tetanus Blade’s poison damage, dormant pathogens within surrounding creatures become reinvigorated. Each creature within 10 feet of you (including you) must succeed on a DC 15 Constitution saving throw or take 14 (4d6) Poison damage and become poisoned until the end of its next turn.

You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. **카구야:** True Strike Divination
Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).
Action Instantaneous Self

**카구야:** Longbow of Melodies Martial Ranged • Slow
This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 기실, 사메하다는 둔검이다. 그러나 그 궤적에는 일체의 빈틈이 없다. 여분의 사이공간을 움직이는 근육들이 뒤쫓는 까닭이다. 그렇기에, 휘두르는 이후에도 타격이 발생하는 기이한 동작이 가능해진다. 그걸 가능케 하는 것은 단 하나의 시동음.
"짓씹어라… ｢사메하다｣."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**라비니아:** Startling Speed 특성
Your movements are so swift that you are almost invisible when in motion. If you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have disadvantage until the start of your next turn. This feature does not function if you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds per day equal to your level.

The primal and ever-changing power of the moon flows through you, granting you the following benefits.Inspired Eclipse. When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.Lunar Vitality. Once per turn when you restore Hit Points to a creature with a spell, you can expend a Bardic Inspiration die and increase the amount of Hit Points restored by a number equal to a roll of the Bardic Inspiration die. The creature’s Speed also increases by 10 feet until the end of its next turn.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

A cleansing stone is a sphere 1 foot in diameter, engraved with mystic sigils. When touching the stone, you can use an action to activate it and remove dirt and grime from your garments and your person. Such stones are often embedded in pedestals in public squares in Aundair or in high-end Ghallanda inns.

You suggest a course of activity—described in no more than 25 words—to one creature you can see within range that can hear and understand you. The suggestion must sound achievable and not involve anything that would obviously deal damage to the target or its allies. For example, you could say, “Fetch the key to the cult’s treasure vault, and give the key to me.” Or you could say, “Stop fighting, leave this library peacefully, and don’t return.” The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or have the Charmed condition for the duration or until you or your allies deal damage to the target. The Charmed target pursues the suggestion to the best of its ability. The suggested activity can continue for the entire duration, but if the suggested activity can be completed in a shorter time, the spell ends for the target upon completing it.

You can perform an esoteric rite for 1 minute. At the end of it, you regain expended Pact Magic spell slots but no more than a number equal to half your maximum (round up). Once you use this feature, you can’t do so again until you finish a Long Rest.

**헤카트리엘:** Death Ward (Saint Vitruvio's Phylactery) Abjuration
You touch a creature and grant it a measure of protection from death. The first time the target would drop to 0 Hit Points before the spell ends, the target instead drops to 1 Hit Point, and the spell ends. If the spell is still in effect when the target is subjected to an effect that would kill it instantly without dealing damage, that effect is negated against the target, and the spell ends.
Targets

**교구장 아로나르:** "느긋한 자들은 그런 해석을 하곤 하지. 하지만 세계수의 의중이란 것은 아무도 모른다. 세계수님은 선택받은 소수를 제외하면 아무에게도 말하지 않으니까."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "겁에 질린 채 칼을 잡은 사람과, 스스로 나선 사람이 같은 결과를 낼 리가 없지."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "네가 선택받았다는 건가?"

**교구장 아로나르:** 엘테라에게 "당연하지만, 아이가 죽기 직전에 구하려고 이렇게 많은 인원이 감시하고 있다."

**교구장 아로나르:** "시험 따위에 귀중한 가호자가 죽어선 안되지."

**엘테라 마스테:** "감시? 하…잘도 가식적인 말을."

**엘테라 마스테:** "노예에게도 같은 방식으로 적용 된다는걸 모르는가 보네…차피 노예나 이 짓거리나 다를게 없어"

**교구장 아로나르:** "그렇다면 너희들에겐 해결책이 있다는 건가?"

**교구장 아로나르:** "싸울 수 있는 사람은 너무나 적은 현실이?"

**카구야:** "그래요. 사람의 생각으로 신의 뜻을 알 수는 없죠. 하지만 그 것이 신의 가호를 이런 식으로 이용해도 된다고 하는 건 아니에요."

**엘테라 마스테:** "내가 알기론 이 룩스테라의 역사는 못해도 몇 천년…"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "적어도 이게 잘못되었다고 단언할 수는 있겠는데."

**엘테라 마스테:** "그 동안 지금까지 사람이 살았다면 차피 너 같은게 없었어도 나서는 자는 이미 있다는 얘기지…이런 노예를 만드는 짓이 아니고 말이야. 무엇보다"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "선택권을 빼앗고 얻는 구원이라면… 그건 구원이 아니야. 착취다."

**엘테라 마스테:** "난 딱히 선악이나 의무 같은 것에 연연해 하는 사람은 아니지만 이건 말해둘 수는 있다…눈 앞에 타인을 휘두르는 자가 있다면 차라리 베는게 낫다고 말이야" @아인스트를 꺼냅니다

**교구장 아로나르:** "내가 악이라면 너희들의 검으로 악을 베어보아라."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Enlarge/Reduce 2nd Level • Transmutation
For the duration, the spell enlarges or reduces a creature or an object you can see within range (see the chosen effect below). A targeted object must be neither worn nor carried. If the target is an unwilling creature, it can make a Constitution saving throw. On a successful save, the spell has no effect. Everything that a targeted creature is wearing and carrying changes size with it. Any item it drops returns to normal size at once. A thrown weapon or piece of ammunition returns to normal size immediately after it hits or misses a target. Enlarge. The target’s size increases by one category—from Medium to Large, for example. The target also has Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its enlarged weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal an extra 1d4 damage on a hit. Reduce. The target’s size decreases by one category—from Medium to Small, for example. The target also has Disadvantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its reduced weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal 1d4 less damage on a hit (this can’t reduce the damage below 1).

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**엘테라 마스테:** Mirror Image 3rd Level • Illusion
Three illusory duplicates of yourself appear in your space. Until the spell ends, the duplicates move with you and mimic your actions, shifting position so it’s impossible to track which image is real. Each time a creature hits you with an attack roll during the spell’s duration, roll a d6 for each of your remaining duplicates. If any of the d6s rolls a 3 or higher, one of the duplicates is hit instead of you, and the duplicate is destroyed. The duplicates otherwise ignore all other damage and effects. The spell ends when all three duplicates are destroyed. A creature is unaffected by this spell if it has the Blinded condition, Blindsight, or Truesight.

**네모(Nemo):** Justice 발동!
당신은 잠시 운명의 저울추를 맞출 수 있는 능력을 얻습니다. 앞으로 8시간 동안, 당신 또는 당신으로부터 60피트 이내에 있는 생명체가 이점 또는 불이익을 적용하여 d20 주사위를 굴리려고 할 때마다, 당신은 반응 행동을 사용하여 해당 주사위 굴림이 이점 또는 불이익의 영향을 받지 않도록 할 수 있습니다.
적군이 유리점을 굴릴 시, 유리점 제거
아군이 불리점을 굴릴 시, 불리점 제거

Choose a willing creature that you can see within range. Until the spell ends, the target’s Speed is doubled, it gains a +2 bonus to Armor Class, it has Advantage on Dexterity saving throws, and it gains an additional action on each of its turns. That action can be used to take only the Attack (one attack only), Dash, Disengage, Hide, or Utilize action. When the spell ends, the target is Incapacitated and has a Speed of 0 until the end of its next turn, as a wave of lethargy washes over it.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

You sting the eyes of a creature attacking you. The target must make a Constitution saving throw (a creature with Blindsight or Immunity to the Blinded condition succeeds automatically). On a failed save, the target has the Blinded condition until the end of the turn. On a successful save, it must subtract 1d4 from the triggering attack roll. The target automatically succeeds on its saves against your subsequent casting of this spell for 24 hours.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Enlarge/Reduce 2nd Level • Transmutation
For the duration, the spell enlarges or reduces a creature or an object you can see within range (see the chosen effect below). A targeted object must be neither worn nor carried. If the target is an unwilling creature, it can make a Constitution saving throw. On a successful save, the spell has no effect. Everything that a targeted creature is wearing and carrying changes size with it. Any item it drops returns to normal size at once. A thrown weapon or piece of ammunition returns to normal size immediately after it hits or misses a target. Enlarge. The target’s size increases by one category—from Medium to Large, for example. The target also has Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its enlarged weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal an extra 1d4 damage on a hit. Reduce. The target’s size decreases by one category—from Medium to Small, for example. The target also has Disadvantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its reduced weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal 1d4 less damage on a hit (this can’t reduce the damage below 1).
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Materials a pinch of powdered iron Concentration V, S, M Action 1 minute 30 ft 1 creature

**Cauldron of Plentiful Resources:** This automation requires the following CPR settings to be enabled to function:
Sync Actor and Token Size

**헤카트리엘:** (와일드서지가 하나 차기는 하는데

**헤카트리엘:** (필요한가?

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Shifting Feature
As a Bonus Action, you can shape-shift to assume a more bestial appearance. This transformation lasts for 1 minute or until you revert to your normal appearance as a Bonus Action. When you shift, you gain Temporary Hit Points equal to 2 times your Proficiency Bonus. You can shift a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. Whenever you shift, you gain the benefit of one of the following options (choose when you select this species) Beasthide. You gain 1d6 additional Temporary Hit Points. While shifted, you have a +1 bonus to your Armor Class. Longtooth. When you shift and as a Bonus Action on your other turns while shifted, you can use your elongated fangs to make an Unarmed Strike. If you hit with this Unarmed Strike and deal damage, you can deal Piercing damage equal to 1d6 plus your Strength modifier, instead of the normal damage of an Unarmed Strike. Swiftstride. While you are shifted, your Speed increases by 10 feet. Additionally, you can move up to 10 feet as a Reaction when a creature ends its turn within 5 feet of you. This reactive movement doesn’t provoke Opportunity Attacks. Wildhunt. While shifted, you have Advantage on Wisdom checks. Additionally, no creature within 30 feet of you can have Advantage on an attack roll against you unless you have the Incapacitated condition.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Special Permanent Self Self

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Shifting Feature
As a Bonus Action, you can shape-shift to assume a more bestial appearance. This transformation lasts for 1 minute or until you revert to your normal appearance as a Bonus Action. When you shift, you gain Temporary Hit Points equal to 2 times your Proficiency Bonus. You can shift a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. Whenever you shift, you gain the benefit of one of the following options (choose when you select this species) Beasthide. You gain 1d6 additional Temporary Hit Points. While shifted, you have a +1 bonus to your Armor Class. Longtooth. When you shift and as a Bonus Action on your other turns while shifted, you can use your elongated fangs to make an Unarmed Strike. If you hit with this Unarmed Strike and deal damage, you can deal Piercing damage equal to 1d6 plus your Strength modifier, instead of the normal damage of an Unarmed Strike. Swiftstride. While you are shifted, your Speed increases by 10 feet. Additionally, you can move up to 10 feet as a Reaction when a creature ends its turn within 5 feet of you. This reactive movement doesn’t provoke Opportunity Attacks. Wildhunt. While shifted, you have Advantage on Wisdom checks. **카구야:** Bardic Inspiration Feature
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Action 1 hour 60 ft 1 creature

**카구야:** Inspired Eclipse Feature
When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.
Targets
카구야 카구야
Bonus Action Instantaneous 30 ft Self

**카구야:** Moon's Inspiration Feature
The primal and ever-changing power of the moon flows through you, granting you the following benefits.Inspired Eclipse. When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.Lunar Vitality. Once per turn when you restore Hit Points to a creature with a spell, you can expend a Bardic Inspiration die and increase the amount of Hit Points restored by a number equal to a roll of the Bardic Inspiration die. The creature’s Speed also increases by 10 feet until the end of its next turn.

**네모(Nemo):** Font of Magic Feature
You can tap into the wellspring of magic within yourself. This wellspring is represented by Sorcery Points, which allow you to create a variety of magical effects. You have 2 Sorcery Points, and you gain more as you reach higher levels, as shown in the Sorcery Points column of the Sorcerer Features table. You can’t have more Sorcery Points than the number shown in the table for your level. You regain all expended Sorcery Points when you finish a Long Rest. You can use your Sorcery Points to fuel the options below, along with other features, such as Metamagic, that use those points. Converting Spell Slots to Sorcery Points. You can expend a spell slot to gain a number of Sorcery Points equal to the slot’s level (no action required). Creating Spell Slots. As a Bonus Action, you can transform unexpended Sorcery Points into one spell slot. The Creating Spell Slots table shows the cost of creating a spell slot of a given level, and it lists the minimum Sorcerer level you must be to create a slot. You can create a spell slot no higher than level 5. Any spell slot you create with this feature vanishes when you finish a Long Rest. Creating Spell Slots Spell Slot Level Sorcery Point Cost Min. **갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

When a creature rolls a d20 for an attack roll against you, you can spend 1 Luck Point to impose Disadvantage on that roll.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword Martial Melee • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) Piercing damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**헤카트리엘:** "가호가 없다는 이유로 등한시한 것이야말로 재능낭비라고?"

**광신자:** "훗… 그런가."

**카구야:** "이 마을 자체도 재정적으로 풍족하지 않아 보여요. 이대로면 아마 마을 자체가 유지되지 않고 뿔뿔이 흩어지겠죠."

**헤카트리엘:** "당당히, 안개에 대항하기 위해 힘쓸 전사들로 삼겠다고 아이들을 모집했어야지."

**헤카트리엘:** "이건 세계수를 태우겠다고 나불거리는 모닥불 애호가들하고 다른 게 없거든?"

**광신자:** "옳은 말이다. 하지만 교구장님께선 다른 길이 없었다고 믿었나보군…"

**광신자:** "우리를 포함해서."

**광신자:** 카구야의 말에는 동의합니다.

**광신자:** "식량조차 수급되지 않는 땅이니까. 어쩔 수 없지."

**헤카트리엘:** "위에 있는 갓 부임한 애는 의욕이 넘치던데."

**헤카트리엘:** "너도 따라와, 저지른 일과 처지를 설명하자."

**카구야:** "축제를 널리 알리고 이 시설을 활용해보죠."

**라비니아:** (그러고보니 교구장도

**라비니아:** (죽었나

**카구야:** "이 시설을 모험가를 훈련시키기 위해 공개한다면 모험가들로부터 지원을 받을 수 있을거에요."

**헤카트리엘:** "안개에 대항하기 위한 전사를 기를 훈련장을 만든 것은 높이 사."

**라비니아:** (반으로 갈라져 죽어

**네모(Nemo):** (아이들과 함께 나오나요?

**헤카트리엘:** "버려지게 두진 말자고."

**Gamemaster:** 소란이 일어나기 전에 우선 마리아만 데리고 나온거로 하죠

**Gamemaster:** 결정되야 제대로 안내해줄 수 있을테니

**광신자:** "…그 말은 나 대신 저기있는 여사제에게 말해주게."

**카구야:** @교구장의 방에서 아까 본 자료를 챙깁니다.

**여사제:** 여러분이 교회로 올라오자 여사제는 당황합니다

**여사제:** "무, 무슨 일이 있던거죠?!"

**카구야:** "좀 긴 이야기가 될 것 같네요."

**라비니아:** "정말로 많은 일들이 있었습니다요"

**카구야:** "그 전에 먼저…"

**헤카트리엘:** "교구장이, 뜻은 옳지만 방법이 그르친 일을 벌이고 있었달까."

**카구야:** @마리아를 앞으로

**여사제:** "…그렇습니까? 교구장님이…"

**네모(Nemo):** (교구장 시체를 가지고 왔으면 보여줍니다.)"교구장과 저 방 안에 있는 사제가 공범입니다.

**헤카트리엘:** "하지만 그렇다고 아무도 찾지 않을 아이들을 잡아들였고."

**라비니아:** "하지만 몇몇은 강제로 잡아들였습니다요"

**헤카트리엘:** "그러지 않으면 미래따위 없을 아이들이라는 핑계로."

**여사제:** 여사제는 마리아를 끌어안은채로 여러분의 이야기를 듣습니다

**여사제:** "설마 그분이 그런 잔인한 짓을…"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "그 설마가 사실이다."

**네모(Nemo):** "만약 마리아가 실종되지 않았다면, 여사제님이 실종신고를 안했다면 지금까지도 납치되었을 겁니다."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "그리고 그 사실은 녀석의 명을 재촉했지."

**여사제:** "이 일은 중앙에 알려야겠어요. 이런 일이 세계수님의 이름으로 자행되고 있었다니…!"

**카구야:** "그건 어려울 것 같아요."

**카구야:** "교구장께서는 중앙과 관계되어 있었습니다."

**여사제:** 여사제가 자료를 읽어보자 손이 떨리는군요

**여사제:** "그럼, 어떻게 해야하죠…?"

**여사제:** "알리지도 못하고, 이대로면 마을은 재정난으로 무너질 운명이라니?"

**헤카트리엘:** @여사제, 잘못을 돌아볼 줄 아는 광신자, 그리고 마리아를 지목합니다.

**헤카트리엘:** "너희 셋이, 이번에는 좀 올바른 방향으로 여길 이끌어 줘야 하겠어."

**헤카트리엘:** "미쳐봤다면, 미친 길이 무엇인지 알고 피할 줄 알겠지?"

**고아 소녀-마리아:** 다들 중요한 이야기 하는 것 같아서 조용히 빠질려고 했는데, 자기 차례라는 표정이군요
